     â”‚ Feature Enhancement Plan: Making Cohere More Engaging                   â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚ Context                                                                 â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚ The user has completed the UI redesign (dark theme, sidebar navigation, â”‚
     â”‚  festival banner) but now finds the platform "too monotonous" and wants â”‚
     â”‚  to add more engaging features.                                         â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚ Current State:                                                          â”‚
     â”‚ - âœ… Core Q&A functionality (questions, answers, voting, tags, search)  â”‚
     â”‚ - âœ… User authentication and profiles                                   â”‚
     â”‚ - âœ… Rich text editor with Tiptap                                       â”‚
     â”‚ - âœ… Reputation system                                                  â”‚
     â”‚ - âœ… Modern UI with dark/light theme                                    â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚ Missing Features (identified from analysis):                            â”‚
     â”‚ - No comments system                                                    â”‚
     â”‚ - No bookmarks/favorites                                                â”‚
     â”‚ - No notifications                                                      â”‚
     â”‚ - No user badges/achievements                                           â”‚
     â”‚ - No code syntax highlighting                                           â”‚
     â”‚ - No related questions                                                  â”‚
     â”‚ - No trending/hot questions                                             â”‚
     â”‚ - No user leaderboard                                                   â”‚
     â”‚ - No advanced search                                                    â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚ The user wants to add features that make the platform more interactive  â”‚
     â”‚ and engaging, similar to Stack Overflow, Reddit, or modern Q&A          â”‚
     â”‚ platforms.                                                              â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚ Recommended Feature Set (Quick Wins - High Impact)                      â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚ Based on the analysis, I recommend implementing these features in       â”‚
     â”‚ priority order:                                                         â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚ Tier 1: Essential Engagement Features (Week 1-2)                        â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚ 1. Bookmarks/Favorites System - Save questions for later                â”‚
     â”‚ 2. Code Syntax Highlighting - Prism.js integration for code blocks      â”‚
     â”‚ 3. User Leaderboard - Top users by reputation                           â”‚
     â”‚ 4. Trending Questions - Hot questions in last 7 days                    â”‚
     â”‚ 5. Related Questions - Show similar questions based on tags             â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚ Tier 2: Social & Interaction Features (Week 3-4)                        â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚ 6. Comments System - Comments on questions and answers                  â”‚
     â”‚ 7. User Badges - Achievement system (First Question, Popular Answer,    â”‚
     â”‚ etc.)                                                                   â”‚
     â”‚ 8. Notifications - In-app notifications for interactions                â”‚
     â”‚ 9. Question Status - Mark as "Solved", "Needs Info", etc.               â”‚
     â”‚ 10. User Mentions - @username tagging in comments                       â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚ Tier 3: Advanced Features (Week 5+)                                     â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚ 11. Advanced Search - Filters by date, author, tags, status             â”‚
     â”‚ 12. Edit History - Track and display content revisions                  â”‚
     â”‚ 13. Flagging System - Report inappropriate content                      â”‚

     â”‚                                                                         â”‚

     â”‚ Backend Changes                                                         â”‚

     â”‚ 1.1 Create Bookmark Model                                               â”‚
     â”‚ New file: server/models/Bookmark.js                                     â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚ const mongoose = require('mongoose');                                   â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚ const bookmarkSchema = new mongoose.Schema({                            â”‚
     â”‚   user: {                                                               â”‚
     â”‚     type: mongoose.Schema.Types.ObjectId,                               â”‚
     â”‚     ref: 'User',                                                        â”‚
     â”‚     required: true                                                      â”‚
     â”‚   },                                                                    â”‚
     â”‚   question: {                                                           â”‚
     â”‚     type: mongoose.Schema.Types.ObjectId,                               â”‚
     â”‚     ref: 'Question',                                                    â”‚
     â”‚     required: true                                                      â”‚
     â”‚   },                                                                    â”‚
     â”‚   createdAt: {                                                          â”‚
     â”‚     type: Date,                                                         â”‚
     â”‚     default: Date.now                                                   â”‚
     â”‚   }                                                                     â”‚
     â”‚ });                                                                     â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚ // Compound index to prevent duplicate bookmarks                        â”‚
     â”‚ bookmarkSchema.index({ user: 1, question: 1 }, { unique: true });       â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚ module.exports = mongoose.model('Bookmark', bookmarkSchema);            â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚

     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚ Add endpoint:                                                           â”‚
     â”‚ // GET /api/users/leaderboard?limit=50&period=all|week|month            â”‚
     â”‚ router.get('/leaderboard', async (req, res) => {                        â”‚
     â”‚   const { limit = 50, period = 'all' } = req.query;                     â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚   let dateFilter = {};                                                  â”‚
     â”‚   if (period === 'week') {                                              â”‚
     â”‚     dateFilter = { createdAt: { $gte: new Date(Date.now() - 7 * 24 * 60 â”‚
     â”‚  * 60 * 1000) } };                                                      â”‚
     â”‚   } else if (period === 'month') {                                      â”‚
     â”‚     dateFilter = { createdAt: { $gte: new Date(Date.now() - 30 * 24 *   â”‚
     â”‚ 60 * 60 * 1000) } };                                                    â”‚
     â”‚   }                                                                     â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚   const users = await User.find()                                       â”‚
     â”‚     .sort({ reputation: -1 })                                           â”‚
     â”‚     .limit(parseInt(limit))                                             â”‚
     â”‚     .select('username avatar reputation createdAt');                    â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚   res.json(users);                                                      â”‚
     â”‚ });                                                                     â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚ 3.2 Create Leaderboard Page                                             â”‚
     â”‚ New file: client/src/pages/Leaderboard.jsx                              â”‚

     â”‚ Display top users with:                                                 â”‚

     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚ 4.1 Create Trending Endpoint                                            â”‚
     â”‚ Modify: server/routes/questions.js                                      â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚ Add endpoint:                                                           â”‚
     â”‚ // GET /api/questions/trending?period=day|week                          â”‚
     â”‚ router.get('/trending', async (req, res) => {                           â”‚
     â”‚   const { period = 'week' } = req.query;                                â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚   const daysAgo = period === 'day' ? 1 : 7;                             â”‚
     â”‚   const dateThreshold = new Date(Date.now() - daysAgo * 24 * 60 * 60 *  â”‚
     â”‚ 1000);                                                                  â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚   const questions = await Question.find({                               â”‚
     â”‚     createdAt: { $gte: dateThreshold }                                  â”‚
     â”‚   })                                                                    â”‚
     â”‚   .populate('author', 'username avatar reputation')                     â”‚
     â”‚   .sort({ views: -1, votes: -1 })                                       â”‚
     â”‚   .limit(20);                                                           â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚   res.json(questions);                                                  â”‚
     â”‚ });                                                                     â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚

     â”‚ 5.1 Create Related Questions Endpoint                                   â”‚
     â”‚ Modify: server/routes/questions.js                                      â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚ Add endpoint:                                                           â”‚
     â”‚ // GET /api/questions/:id/related                                       â”‚
     â”‚ router.get('/:id/related', async (req, res) => {                        â”‚
     â”‚   const question = await Question.findById(req.params.id);              â”‚
     â”‚   if (!question) return res.status(404).json({ message: 'Question not   â”‚
     â”‚ found' });                                                              â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚   // Find questions with overlapping tags                               â”‚
     â”‚   const related = await Question.find({                                 â”‚
     â”‚     _id: { $ne: question._id },                                         â”‚
     â”‚     tags: { $in: question.tags }                                        â”‚
     â”‚   })                                                                    â”‚
     â”‚   .populate('author', 'username avatar')                                â”‚
     â”‚   .sort({ votes: -1, views: -1 })                                       â”‚
     â”‚   .limit(5);                                                            â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚   res.json(related);                                                    â”‚
     â”‚ });                                                                     â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚

     â”‚ 6.1 Create Comment Model                                                â”‚
     â”‚ New file: server/models/Comment.js                                      â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚ const mongoose = require('mongoose');                                   â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚ const commentSchema = new mongoose.Schema({                             â”‚
     â”‚   body: {                                                               â”‚
     â”‚     type: String,                                                       â”‚
     â”‚     required: true,                                                     â”‚
     â”‚     maxlength: 500                                                      â”‚
     â”‚   },                                                                    â”‚
     â”‚   author: {                                                             â”‚
     â”‚     type: mongoose.Schema.Types.ObjectId,                               â”‚
     â”‚     ref: 'User',                                                        â”‚
     â”‚     required: true                                                      â”‚
     â”‚   },                                                                    â”‚
     â”‚   targetType: {                                                         â”‚
     â”‚     type: String,                                                       â”‚
     â”‚     enum: ['Question', 'Answer'],                                       â”‚
     â”‚     required: true                                                      â”‚
     â”‚   },                                                                    â”‚
     â”‚   targetId: {                                                           â”‚
     â”‚     type: mongoose.Schema.Types.ObjectId,                               â”‚
     â”‚     required: true                                                      â”‚
     â”‚   },                                                                    â”‚
     â”‚   votes: {                                                              â”‚
     â”‚     type: Number,                                                       â”‚
     â”‚     default: 0                                                          â”‚
     â”‚   },                                                                    â”‚
     â”‚   createdAt: {                                                          â”‚
     â”‚     type: Date,                                                         â”‚
     â”‚     default: Date.now                                                   â”‚
     â”‚   },                                                                    â”‚
     â”‚   updatedAt: {                                                          â”‚
     â”‚     type: Date,                                                         â”‚
     â”‚     default: Date.now                                                   â”‚
     â”‚   }                                                                     â”‚
     â”‚ });                                                                     â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚ commentSchema.index({ targetType: 1, targetId: 1, createdAt: -1 });     â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚ module.exports = mongoose.model('Comment', commentSchema);              â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚

     â”‚   recipient: {                                                          â”‚
     â”‚     type: mongoose.Schema.Types.ObjectId,                               â”‚
     â”‚     ref: 'User',                                                        â”‚
     â”‚     required: true                                                      â”‚

     â”‚   type: {                                                               â”‚

     â”‚     required: true                                                      â”‚

     â”‚ 9.1 Update Question Model                                               â”‚
     â”‚ Modify: server/models/Question.js                                       â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚ Add status field:                                                       â”‚
     â”‚ status: {                                                               â”‚
     â”‚   type: String,                                                         â”‚
     â”‚   enum: ['open', 'solved', 'needs_info', 'closed'],                     â”‚
     â”‚   default: 'open'                                                       â”‚
     â”‚ }                                                                       â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚ 9.2 Update Question Routes                                              â”‚
     â”‚ Modify: server/routes/questions.js                                      â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚ Add endpoint:                                                           â”‚
     â”‚ // PUT /api/questions/:id/status                                        â”‚
     â”‚ router.put('/:id/status', auth, async (req, res) => {                   â”‚
     â”‚   const { status } = req.body;                                          â”‚
     â”‚   const question = await Question.findById(req.params.id);              â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚   if (!question) return res.status(404).json({ message: 'Question not   â”‚
     â”‚ found' });                                                              â”‚
     â”‚   if (question.author.toString() !== req.userId) {                      â”‚
     â”‚     return res.status(403).json({ message: 'Not authorized' });         â”‚
     â”‚   }                                                                     â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚   question.status = status;                                             â”‚
     â”‚   await question.save();                                                â”‚
     â”‚   res.json(question);                                                   â”‚
     â”‚ });                                                                     â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚

     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚ - Database Migrations: No migrations needed (MongoDB is schemaless),    â”‚

     â”‚ recipient+read for notifications)                                       â”‚
     â”‚ - Real-time: Notifications are not real-time (require page refresh),    â”‚
     â”‚ consider WebSocket for future                                           â”‚
     â”‚ - Rate Limiting: Add rate limiting to prevent spam (comments, votes)    â”‚
     â”‚ - Caching: Consider caching leaderboard and trending queries (Redis or  â”‚
     â”‚ in-memory)                                                              â”‚
     â”‚ - Email Notifications: Phase 2 feature, requires email service          â”‚
     â”‚ (SendGrid, Mailgun)                                                     â”‚
     â”‚ - Mobile: All features should be responsive and work on mobile devices  â”‚
     â”‚ - Accessibility: Add ARIA labels, keyboard navigation, screen reader    â”‚

     â”‚ New file: server/models/Bookmark.js                                     â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚ const mongoose = require('mongoose');                                   â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚ const bookmarkSchema = new mongoose.Schema({                            â”‚
     â”‚   user: {                                                               â”‚
     â”‚     type: mongoose.Schema.Types.ObjectId,                               â”‚
     â”‚     ref: 'User',                                                        â”‚
     â”‚     required: true                                                      â”‚
     â”‚   },                                                                    â”‚
     â”‚   question: {                                                           â”‚
     â”‚     type: mongoose.Schema.Types.ObjectId,                               â”‚
     â”‚     ref: 'Question',                                                    â”‚
     â”‚     required: true                                                      â”‚
     â”‚   },                                                                    â”‚
     â”‚   createdAt: {                                                          â”‚
     â”‚     type: Date,                                                         â”‚
     â”‚     default: Date.now                                                   â”‚
     â”‚   }                                                                     â”‚
     â”‚ });                                                                     â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚ // Compound index to prevent duplicate bookmarks                        â”‚
     â”‚ bookmarkSchema.index({ user: 1, question: 1 }, { unique: true });       â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚ module.exports = mongoose.model('Bookmark', bookmarkSchema);            â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚

     â”‚ Phase 3: User Leaderboard (Day 4)                                       â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚ 3.1 Create Leaderboard Endpoint                                         â”‚
     â”‚ Modify: server/routes/users.js                                          â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚ Add endpoint:                                                           â”‚
     â”‚ // GET /api/users/leaderboard?limit=50&period=all|week|month            â”‚
     â”‚ router.get('/leaderboard', async (req, res) => {                        â”‚
     â”‚   const { limit = 50, period = 'all' } = req.query;                     â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚   let dateFilter = {};                                                  â”‚
     â”‚   if (period === 'week') {                                              â”‚
     â”‚     dateFilter = { createdAt: { $gte: new Date(Date.now() - 7 * 24 * 60 â”‚
     â”‚  * 60 * 1000) } };                                                      â”‚
     â”‚   } else if (period === 'month') {                                      â”‚
     â”‚     dateFilter = { createdAt: { $gte: new Date(Date.now() - 30 * 24 *   â”‚
     â”‚ 60 * 60 * 1000) } };                                                    â”‚
     â”‚   }                                                                     â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚   const users = await User.find()                                       â”‚
     â”‚     .sort({ reputation: -1 })                                           â”‚
     â”‚     .limit(parseInt(limit))                                             â”‚
     â”‚     .select('username avatar reputation createdAt');                    â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚   res.json(users);                                                      â”‚
     â”‚ });                                                                     â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚ 3.2 Create Leaderboard Page                                             â”‚
     â”‚ New file: client/src/pages/Leaderboard.jsx                              â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚

     â”‚ - Rank, avatar, username, reputation                                    â”‚

     â”‚ Modify: client/src/components/Sidebar.jsx                               â”‚

     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚ Phase 4: Trending Questions (Day 5)                                     â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚ 4.1 Create Trending Endpoint                                            â”‚
     â”‚ Modify: server/routes/questions.js                                      â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚ Add endpoint:                                                           â”‚
     â”‚ // GET /api/questions/trending?period=day|week                          â”‚
     â”‚ router.get('/trending', async (req, res) => {                           â”‚
     â”‚   const { period = 'week' } = req.query;                                â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚   const daysAgo = period === 'day' ? 1 : 7;                             â”‚
     â”‚   const dateThreshold = new Date(Date.now() - daysAgo * 24 * 60 * 60 *  â”‚
     â”‚ 1000);                                                                  â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚   const questions = await Question.find({                               â”‚
     â”‚     createdAt: { $gte: dateThreshold }                                  â”‚
     â”‚   })                                                                    â”‚
     â”‚   .populate('author', 'username avatar reputation')                     â”‚
     â”‚   .sort({ views: -1, votes: -1 })                                       â”‚
     â”‚   .limit(20);                                                           â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚   res.json(questions);                                                  â”‚
     â”‚ });                                                                     â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚ 4.2 Add Trending Section to Home Page                                   â”‚
     â”‚ Modify: client/src/pages/Home.jsx                                       â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚ Add "Trending This Week" section in sidebar or above question list      â”‚
     â”‚ with:                                                                   â”‚
     â”‚ - Top 5 trending questions                                              â”‚
     â”‚ - View count and vote count                                             â”‚
     â”‚ - Compact card design                                                   â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚ Phase 5: Related Questions (Day 6)                                      â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚ 5.1 Create Related Questions Endpoint                                   â”‚
     â”‚ Modify: server/routes/questions.js                                      â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚ Add endpoint:                                                           â”‚
     â”‚ // GET /api/questions/:id/related                                       â”‚
     â”‚ router.get('/:id/related', async (req, res) => {                        â”‚
     â”‚   const question = await Question.findById(req.params.id);              â”‚
     â”‚   if (!question) return res.status(404).json({ message: 'Question not   â”‚
     â”‚ found' });                                                              â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚   // Find questions with overlapping tags                               â”‚
     â”‚   const related = await Question.find({                                 â”‚
     â”‚     _id: { $ne: question._id },                                         â”‚
     â”‚     tags: { $in: question.tags }                                        â”‚
     â”‚   })                                                                    â”‚
     â”‚   .populate('author', 'username avatar')                                â”‚
     â”‚   .sort({ votes: -1, views: -1 })                                       â”‚
     â”‚   .limit(5);                                                            â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚   res.json(related);                                                    â”‚
     â”‚ });                                                                     â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚

     â”‚ const mongoose = require('mongoose');                                   â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚ const notificationSchema = new mongoose.Schema({                        â”‚
     â”‚   recipient: {                                                          â”‚
     â”‚     type: mongoose.Schema.Types.ObjectId,                               â”‚
     â”‚     ref: 'User',                                                        â”‚
     â”‚     required: true                                                      â”‚

     â”‚   type: {                                                               â”‚

     â”‚     enum: ['answer', 'comment', 'vote', 'mention', 'badge'],            â”‚
     â”‚     required: true                                                      â”‚
     â”‚   },                                                                    â”‚
     â”‚   actor: {                                                              â”‚
     â”‚     type: mongoose.Schema.Types.ObjectId,                               â”‚
     â”‚     ref: 'User'                                                         â”‚
     â”‚   },                                                                    â”‚
     â”‚   targetType: {                                                         â”‚
     â”‚     type: String,                                                       â”‚
     â”‚     enum: ['Question', 'Answer', 'Comment']                             â”‚
     â”‚   },                                                                    â”‚
     â”‚   targetId: {                                                           â”‚
     â”‚     type: mongoose.Schema.Types.ObjectId                                â”‚
     â”‚   },                                                                    â”‚
     â”‚   message: String,                                                      â”‚
     â”‚   read: {                                                               â”‚
     â”‚     type: Boolean,                                                      â”‚
     â”‚     default: false                                                      â”‚
     â”‚   },                                                                    â”‚
     â”‚   createdAt: {                                                          â”‚
     â”‚     type: Date,                                                         â”‚
     â”‚     default: Date.now                                                   â”‚
     â”‚   }                                                                     â”‚
     â”‚ });                                                                     â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚ notificationSchema.index({ recipient: 1, read: 1, createdAt: -1 });     â”‚

     â”‚ Modify: server/models/Question.js                                       â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚ Add status field:                                                       â”‚
     â”‚ status: {                                                               â”‚
     â”‚   type: String,                                                         â”‚
     â”‚   enum: ['open', 'solved', 'needs_info', 'closed'],                     â”‚
     â”‚   default: 'open'                                                       â”‚
     â”‚ }                                                                       â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚ 9.2 Update Question Routes                                              â”‚
     â”‚ Modify: server/routes/questions.js                                      â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚ Add endpoint:                                                           â”‚
     â”‚ // PUT /api/questions/:id/status                                        â”‚
     â”‚ router.put('/:id/status', auth, async (req, res) => {                   â”‚
     â”‚   const { status } = req.body;                                          â”‚
     â”‚   const question = await Question.findById(req.params.id);              â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚   if (!question) return res.status(404).json({ message: 'Question not   â”‚
     â”‚ found' });                                                              â”‚
     â”‚   if (question.author.toString() !== req.userId) {                      â”‚
     â”‚     return res.status(403).json({ message: 'Not authorized' });         â”‚
     â”‚   }                                                                     â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚   question.status = status;                                             â”‚
     â”‚   await question.save();                                                â”‚
     â”‚   res.json(question);                                                   â”‚
     â”‚ });                                                                     â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚

     â”‚ Implementation Notes                                                    â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚ - Database Migrations: No migrations needed (MongoDB is schemaless),    â”‚
     â”‚ but seed new badge data                                                 â”‚
     â”‚ - Performance: Add indexes on new models (user+question for bookmarks,  â”‚
     â”‚ recipient+read for notifications)                                       â”‚
     â”‚ - Real-time: Notifications are not real-time (require page refresh),    â”‚
     â”‚ consider WebSocket for future                                           â”‚
     â”‚ - Rate Limiting: Add rate limiting to prevent spam (comments, votes)    â”‚
     â”‚ - Caching: Consider caching leaderboard and trending queries (Redis or  â”‚
     â”‚ in-memory)                                                              â”‚
     â”‚ - Email Notifications: Phase 2 feature, requires email service          â”‚
     â”‚ (SendGrid, Mailgun)                                                     â”‚
     â”‚ - Mobile: All features should be responsive and work on mobile devices  â”‚
     â”‚ - Accessibility: Add ARIA labels, keyboard navigation, screen reader    â”‚
     â”‚ support                                                                 â”‚
     â”‚ - Testing: Write unit tests for badge service, notification service     â”‚
     â”‚ - Documentation: Update API.md with new endpoints                       â”‚

     â”‚ New file: server/models/Bookmark.js                                     â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚ const mongoose = require('mongoose');                                   â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚ const bookmarkSchema = new mongoose.Schema({                            â”‚
     â”‚   user: {                                                               â”‚
     â”‚     type: mongoose.Schema.Types.ObjectId,                               â”‚
     â”‚     ref: 'User',                                                        â”‚
     â”‚     required: true                                                      â”‚
     â”‚   },                                                                    â”‚
     â”‚   question: {                                                           â”‚
     â”‚     type: mongoose.Schema.Types.ObjectId,                               â”‚
     â”‚     ref: 'Question',                                                    â”‚
     â”‚     required: true                                                      â”‚
     â”‚   },                                                                    â”‚
     â”‚   createdAt: {                                                          â”‚
     â”‚     type: Date,                                                         â”‚
     â”‚     default: Date.now                                                   â”‚
     â”‚   }                                                                     â”‚
     â”‚ });                                                                     â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚ // Compound index to prevent duplicate bookmarks                        â”‚
     â”‚ bookmarkSchema.index({ user: 1, question: 1 }, { unique: true });       â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚ module.exports = mongoose.model('Bookmark', bookmarkSchema);            â”‚

     â”‚ Phase 3: User Leaderboard (Day 4)                                       â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚ 3.1 Create Leaderboard Endpoint                                         â”‚
     â”‚ Modify: server/routes/users.js                                          â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚ Add endpoint:                                                           â”‚
     â”‚ // GET /api/users/leaderboard?limit=50&period=all|week|month            â”‚
     â”‚ router.get('/leaderboard', async (req, res) => {                        â”‚
     â”‚   const { limit = 50, period = 'all' } = req.query;                     â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚   let dateFilter = {};                                                  â”‚
     â”‚   if (period === 'week') {                                              â”‚
     â”‚     dateFilter = { createdAt: { $gte: new Date(Date.now() - 7 * 24 * 60 â”‚
     â”‚  * 60 * 1000) } };                                                      â”‚
     â”‚   } else if (period === 'month') {                                      â”‚
     â”‚     dateFilter = { createdAt: { $gte: new Date(Date.now() - 30 * 24 *   â”‚
     â”‚ 60 * 60 * 1000) } };                                                    â”‚
     â”‚   }                                                                     â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚   const users = await User.find()                                       â”‚
     â”‚     .sort({ reputation: -1 })                                           â”‚
     â”‚     .limit(parseInt(limit))                                             â”‚
     â”‚     .select('username avatar reputation createdAt');                    â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚   res.json(users);                                                      â”‚
     â”‚ });                                                                     â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚

     â”‚ Modify: server/routes/questions.js                                      â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚ Add endpoint:                                                           â”‚
     â”‚ // GET /api/questions/trending?period=day|week                          â”‚
     â”‚ router.get('/trending', async (req, res) => {                           â”‚
     â”‚   const { period = 'week' } = req.query;                                â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚   const daysAgo = period === 'day' ? 1 : 7;                             â”‚
     â”‚   const dateThreshold = new Date(Date.now() - daysAgo * 24 * 60 * 60 *  â”‚
     â”‚ 1000);                                                                  â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚   const questions = await Question.find({                               â”‚
     â”‚     createdAt: { $gte: dateThreshold }                                  â”‚
     â”‚   })                                                                    â”‚
     â”‚   .populate('author', 'username avatar reputation')                     â”‚
     â”‚   .sort({ views: -1, votes: -1 })                                       â”‚
     â”‚   .limit(20);                                                           â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚   res.json(questions);                                                  â”‚
     â”‚ });                                                                     â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚

     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚ 5.1 Create Related Questions Endpoint                                   â”‚
     â”‚ Modify: server/routes/questions.js                                      â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚ Add endpoint:                                                           â”‚
     â”‚ // GET /api/questions/:id/related                                       â”‚
     â”‚ router.get('/:id/related', async (req, res) => {                        â”‚
     â”‚   const question = await Question.findById(req.params.id);              â”‚
     â”‚   if (!question) return res.status(404).json({ message: 'Question not   â”‚
     â”‚ found' });                                                              â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚   // Find questions with overlapping tags                               â”‚
     â”‚   const related = await Question.find({                                 â”‚
     â”‚     _id: { $ne: question._id },                                         â”‚
     â”‚     tags: { $in: question.tags }                                        â”‚
     â”‚   })                                                                    â”‚
     â”‚   .populate('author', 'username avatar')                                â”‚
     â”‚   .sort({ votes: -1, views: -1 })                                       â”‚
     â”‚   .limit(5);                                                            â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚   res.json(related);                                                    â”‚
     â”‚ });                                                                     â”‚

     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚ const mongoose = require('mongoose');                                   â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚ const notificationSchema = new mongoose.Schema({                        â”‚
     â”‚   recipient: {                                                          â”‚
     â”‚     type: mongoose.Schema.Types.ObjectId,                               â”‚
     â”‚     ref: 'User',                                                        â”‚
     â”‚     required: true                                                      â”‚
     â”‚   },                                                                    â”‚
     â”‚   type: {                                                               â”‚

     â”‚     required: true                                                      â”‚
     â”‚   },                                                                    â”‚
     â”‚   actor: {                                                              â”‚
     â”‚     type: mongoose.Schema.Types.ObjectId,                               â”‚
     â”‚     ref: 'User'                                                         â”‚
     â”‚   },                                                                    â”‚
     â”‚   targetType: {                                                         â”‚
     â”‚     type: String,                                                       â”‚
     â”‚     enum: ['Question', 'Answer', 'Comment']                             â”‚
     â”‚   },                                                                    â”‚

     â”‚     type: mongoose.Schema.Types.ObjectId                                â”‚
     â”‚   },                                                                    â”‚
     â”‚   message: String,                                                      â”‚
     â”‚   read: {                                                               â”‚
     â”‚     type: Boolean,                                                      â”‚
     â”‚     default: false                                                      â”‚
     â”‚   },                                                                    â”‚
     â”‚   createdAt: {                                                          â”‚
     â”‚     type: Date,                                                         â”‚
     â”‚     default: Date.now                                                   â”‚
     â”‚   }                                                                     â”‚
     â”‚ });                                                                     â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚ notificationSchema.index({ recipient: 1, read: 1, createdAt: -1 });     â”‚

     â”‚ 9.1 Update Question Model                                               â”‚
     â”‚ Modify: server/models/Question.js                                       â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚ Add status field:                                                       â”‚
     â”‚ status: {                                                               â”‚
     â”‚   type: String,                                                         â”‚
     â”‚   enum: ['open', 'solved', 'needs_info', 'closed'],                     â”‚
     â”‚   default: 'open'                                                       â”‚
     â”‚ }                                                                       â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚ 9.2 Update Question Routes                                              â”‚
     â”‚ Modify: server/routes/questions.js                                      â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚ Add endpoint:                                                           â”‚
     â”‚ // PUT /api/questions/:id/status                                        â”‚
     â”‚ router.put('/:id/status', auth, async (req, res) => {                   â”‚
     â”‚   const { status } = req.body;                                          â”‚
     â”‚   const question = await Question.findById(req.params.id);              â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚   if (!question) return res.status(404).json({ message: 'Question not   â”‚
     â”‚ found' });                                                              â”‚
     â”‚   if (question.author.toString() !== req.userId) {                      â”‚
     â”‚     return res.status(403).json({ message: 'Not authorized' });         â”‚
     â”‚   }                                                                     â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚   question.status = status;                                             â”‚
     â”‚   await question.save();                                                â”‚
     â”‚   res.json(question);                                                   â”‚
     â”‚ });                                                                     â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚ 9.3 Add Status Badge to QuestionCard                                    â”‚

     â”‚ Add status badge (âœ… Solved, â“ Needs Info, ğŸ”’ Closed) in card header.  â”‚

     â”‚ Implementation Notes                                                    â”‚
     â”‚                                                                         â”‚
     â”‚ - Database Migrations: No migrations needed (MongoDB is schemaless),    â”‚
     â”‚ but seed new badge data                                                 â”‚
     â”‚ - Performance: Add indexes on new models (user+question for bookmarks,  â”‚
     â”‚ recipient+read for notifications)                                       â”‚
     â”‚ - Real-time: Notifications are not real-time (require page refresh),    â”‚
     â”‚ consider WebSocket for future                                           â”‚
     â”‚ - Rate Limiting: Add rate limiting to prevent spam (comments, votes)    â”‚
     â”‚ - Caching: Consider caching leaderboard and trending queries (Redis or  â”‚
     â”‚ in-memory)                                                              â”‚
     â”‚ - Email Notifications: Phase 2 feature, requires email service          â”‚
     â”‚ (SendGrid, Mailgun)                                                     â”‚
     â”‚ - Mobile: All features should be responsive and work on mobile devices  â”‚
     â”‚ - Accessibility: Add ARIA labels, keyboard navigation, screen reader    â”‚
     â”‚ support                                                                 â”‚
